I'm so happy with the service I received at this dental office! The front desk is very professional and signed me in very quickly, with no hassles. I'm used to the spacers (in the mouth) during the X-ray digging into my tongue or gums, but I've never had a more painless X-ray experience in my life. The staff is extremely friendly and professional and made me feel very comfortable thoughout the entire treatment. I also felt that my cleaning was very thorough.

Dr. Yun did a fantastic job with my tooth fillings. I never felt any pain when the numbing was injected into my gums and the actual filling process was quick and painless too. Highly recommend this place!<//Text>

<rate>5</rate><date>1557635960734</date><Name>Ipshita Datta< /Name>< Review>
The trail from the Vista point to slacker Hill was moderately intensive and we loved the hike. Specially near the slacker ridge, about 1 mile from the start, the wind gets intense and could literally blow you off. But a few meters ahead, the trail ascends to a beautiful view. Loved the hike and would come back again.

Mind it, this trail is less travelled, so u can trudge at a decent pace and reach the top in about 45-50 mins, watch out for the steep ascends ... Hydrate and take in the view...</Review>

< Review>
It is one of the best spot to view San Francisco and Golden Gate Bridge. The hike is only about 0.4 miles, but the elevation is over 300 feet. You may also go down to the front side slope to find good spots for photography. When I was up there today (4/21/19), it was windy. Today is only for scouting, I will definitely come back. If you have hiking sticks, bring them.< /Review>

<rating>5<//rating>< text>
I had heard about Slackers Hill and it being the hidden gem of the Bay!  I decided to fly my girlfriend and I on a trip to SF Bay.  I had it planned for us to go for a run down the bay, across the Golden Gate, and up the trail to Slackers Hill.  This is where I proposed to my now wife in marriage.  It was the most beautiful and secluded place to view the Bay.  A hidden gem it is!!!  It was a clear Oct. 9, and her birthday!  Now when we see pictures of the Golden Gate Bridge, we see Slackers Hill overlooking the bridge, the place where we had a very special moment in our life!<//text>

<Review>I spent about six months researching tattoo artists before settling on Ian Jones at True Tattoo. Looking at his work it was closest to what I wanted. I had always wanted an arm sleeve, and had a good idea of what I wanted. My initial meeting with Ian was fantastic. He's a wonderful artist and listened to me carefully, asked for as many notes that I could provide and also photo examples of what I liked and also what I didn't like. On the second visit we mapped out the entire sleeve in terms of what artwork would go where, and he got to work. The entire process beginning to end was extremely collaborative, and that's what I liked. I made it clear from the offset that my goal was to get the entire sleeve done very quickly, and 7 weeks and 5 sessions later I was done. Scheduling was very easy and he was always on time, and ready to go. He was also very flexible as one time I had to delay a session due to a work meeting, and he made it work. I love his artwork, his attention to detail and his process. It put me at ease right away that when stenciling a portion of the tattoo that he would remove and restart multiple times if he wasn't happy with the placement or layout. He would always have me look at the stencil, and take some time for the concept to sink in before making sure I was 100% happy with it. I couldn't recommend Ian and True Tattoo more. A fantastic experience beginning to end.< /Review>< pics>

< username>
tori holder<//username>
<time>1413954181332< /time><rate>5</rate>< Text>
Had a great experience here. They are punctual (I arrived on time for my appointment and did not have to wait). The staff is very friendly while being super professional, I felt completely at home and relaxed, which is something I don't say often. Not only do they uphold all necessary health/safety standards, they are very straightforward about this and take pride in showing you all materials to be used and keeping everything very orderly (this is a really big deal to me, I need to see the needle come out of the packaging and go in a disposal container and know all hands have been washed, etc). While I had talked about the tattoo I was going to get with the artist before I went in, when I got there and we actually got to pointing-at-the-area placement we realized where I had been planning on was not ideal for longevity/possibility of distortion. The artist explained this to me in full, suggested several good nearby placements, and said ultimately the decision was mine but wanted me to make an informed decision as opposed to not knowing, and to take all the time I needed to think about this, whether in shop or rescheduling to a later date. I went with one of the alternate locations that was just a few inches from the original spot (we actually put the template for the tattoo on the location and I was encouraged to look at it in the mirror a bit to make sure it worked for me before we started) and am very pleased with how it turned out, but it was this level of "your body, your decision, no pressure" that I think is essential in any establishment, especially one where you have the product for forever. Also, they thoroughly go through the healing care with you and provide a very detailed printout of post tattoo care and bandage you up really well. And of course while I have so emphasized the clean and safe elements, of course the artists are super talented and the old-school tattoo parlor vibe is in full effect. Definitely recommending this to anyone looking for a place to have their next tattoo done.<//Text>

<Resp>None< /Resp><gmap_id>0x54cde55d4891ec1d:0x42c765616470e0eb< /gmap_id>< text>
A good place to camp in privacy. Enough space for two cars and two tents. There's a table and a fire place with lots of wood lying around. Best part is that this site is walking distance from Castle lake and a bunch of hiking trails. Remember this is not a reservation based site. First come, first serve. There's no fresh water available. But there is a stream passing by. There are a couple of washrooms on site but with no water and hardly any maintenance. Overall a very good camp site with a few amenities.<//text>

< review>
This is one of those restaurants where you need to go casually dressed and all hands in,,,,,because it is messy and you will get some of the spices (and food) on yourself. The servings come out piping hot in a plastic bag (this is where I removed one star - why not have a paper bag) which you dump onto your paper covered table. You use your hands to dig in. I have been to this restaurant about 3 times so far - ordered the king crab legs and gumbo soup once; the Cajun crawfish and sweet potato fries the second and the spicy Cajun prawns the third. The seafood is good - crab of course needs to be worked on - the others less so. I wish they had more flavors than they do but what they offer is good. Usually I go for the Cajun or garlic seasonings and a single order of 1 lb of seafood is enough.<//review>

< Review>
Really painful to throw down $10 for the Michelada but in my opinion it's worth it if you are there for a celebration. They sell the king crab legs by the pound and will not include a 4th leg for an extra charge if you're there with a party of four, they ONLY come in packs of 3 so you'll be required to share the bounty or Fork over another $29 for a 3 pack. Also they bring the food out as it is cooked so don't anticipate eating every plate all together as a family. In my opinion it's better to get stuff that you can share. I would have given five stars if the floor wasn't sticky and the soap dispenser was empty in the bathroom (if you get king crab legs you will be heading to the bathroom immediately upon finishing) also I wish they had an option to give you an extra king crab leg. The food was excellent the portions were great I'll be at the price was a little high.</Review>

Awesome food! Seriously, best seafood in a bag, the seasoning is amazing and it's so flavorful. My only concern is that they asked for my ID, which sure they can ask for your ID, but they cannot refuse to accept your credit card if you choose not to show it or even if the name doesn't match. That's per Visa and Mastercards regulations. In CA you don't need an ID to get a credit card. The manager Oscar and even the waitress didn't want to accept my Visa credit card, they asked to see my social media accounts to verify it's me (odd because my full name isn't used) they even stood right in front of the exit end of my booth like I was a criminal going to attempt an escape (my fiance put our 2 yr old in the car and I had my daughter with me). I'm a teacher, I'm not going to lose my career of stupidity. They seemed very unprofessional asking for my social media and I didn't appreciate the service I received just because I left my ID at home an hour away! They also scared my daughter over this whole ID issue. So if you eat there you will enjoy the food, but make sure you bring your ID or they might hold you hostage. I will be following up with Visa about this incident, it's not right. IDs are a way of tracking people, there is no law saying you HAVE TO HAVE AN ID just like you don't need one to get a credit card and I'm definitely going to take this matter as far as I can. <review>To whom it may concern:
Dear boiling crab or corporate owners,

<Time>1538537422030< /Time><rate>5</rate><review>A messy, delicious experience for the whole family. My family of five all had the shrimp, it was served in bags (the restaurant menu states that this is to preserve the flavor of the seasonings) and the amount in each was up to the person ordering. The minimum is half a pound which was perfect for my 8 and 9 year olds. My 13 year old, my wife and myself all got a pound of shrimp each and it was just right. Of course your mileage may vary. You can have the shrimp cooked with a variety of seasonings, but I recommend the whole shabang, it's a tasty mix of all their seasonings. The last decision is if you want your shrimps spicy. My family went for the mild and they all loved it, just enough kick my wife said, I had the medium and it was hot but enjoyable. For those feeling adventurous, they have the XXX level of spicy which according to the waiter, is a 10 on a scale of 1-10.  Anyway, delicious shrimp and a whole lot more seafood on the menu. <Rating>3< /Rating>< Text>
Service: It was our first time, so the waitress guided us in terms how to order the dishes. She recommended us to order medium spicy because it was spicy for everyone. But I would prefer spicy because medium was blend for me.
Food- We ordered the dungeons crabs which were expensive. And got one lbs. shrimp the "sha bang style". It has tons of oil in the sauce so if you are health freak not a good place to eat. Over all the food tasted okay with medium sauce.
Price -  Crabs are expensive because of the season.
Restaurant - You cannot use forks and knives here. If you don't like using hands then not the right place to be. You will be given a bib because the hands get dirty and you may spill while eating crabs. Overall food was good. Bathroom wasn't clean and no toilet papers.
Overall experience - Once in a blue moon nice set of place to hang out with friends and enjoy the talks and music in background.</Text>
